namespace = d_law_tec
#法律
d_law_tec.700 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_laws
	flavor = daoyu_laws_flavor
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_ruler_speaking_to_people.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/leader_speaking_to_a_group_of_people"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
		if = {
			limit = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
			random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.700 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_target_country#重新选目标
		trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.700 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_modify_no_target_country
		trigger = { not = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.710 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_modify_target_country
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.720 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_modify_our_country
		random_country = { limit = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		add_modifier = { name = daoyu_target_country days = 1 }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.720 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.10 popup = yes } }
	}
}

	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_laws
	flavor = daoyu_laws_flavor

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/leader_speaking_to_a_group_of_people"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
		if = {
			limit = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
			random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.710 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NO_OBJECTIVE#你未选择目标
		trigger = { not = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { d_law_tec.710 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_target_country#重新选目标

		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { d_law_tec.710 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_modify_target_country
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.720 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.700 popup = yes } }
	}
}

	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }

		}
	}
	option = {
		name = POWER_STRUCTURE#权力结构
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.730 popup = yes } }

		name = ECONOMY#经济

	}

		name = RESIGN

	}
}
#权力结构
d_law_tec.730 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = LAWS
	desc = POWER_STRUCTURE
	flavor = daoyu_laws_desc
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_ruler_speaking_to_people.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/leader_speaking_to_a_group_of_people"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { set_variable = d_law_tec_730 }
	option = {
		name = lawgroup_governance_principles#治理原则
		trigger = { daoyu_activate_law_trigger = yes }
		set_global_variable = lawgroup_governance_principles
	}
	option = {
		name = law_chiefdom
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_chiefdom } has_global_variable = lawgroup_governance_principles is_country_type = decentralized } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_chiefdom }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_monarchy
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_monarchy } has_global_variable = lawgroup_governance_principles not = { has_law = law_type:law_anarchy } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_monarchy }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_presidential_republic
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic } has_global_variable = lawgroup_governance_principles has_technology_researched = democracy } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_parliamentary_republic
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic } has_global_variable = lawgroup_governance_principles has_technology_researched = democracy } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_theocracy
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_theocracy } has_global_variable = lawgroup_governance_principles } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_theocracy }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_council_republic
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_council_republic has_law = law_type:law_hereditary_bureaucrats } has_global_variable = lawgroup_governance_principles has_technology_researched = socialism } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_council_republic }
	}
	option = {
		name = lawgroup_distribution_of_power#权力分配
		trigger = { daoyu_activate_law_trigger = yes }
		set_global_variable = lawgroup_distribution_of_power
	}
	option = {
		name = law_autocracy
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_autocracy } has_global_variable = lawgroup_distribution_of_power not = { has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_autocracy }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_technocracy
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_technocracy } has_global_variable = lawgroup_distribution_of_power has_technology_researched = central_archives } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_technocracy }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_oligarchy
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy } has_global_variable = lawgroup_distribution_of_power } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_oligarchy }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_elder_council
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_elder_council } has_global_variable = lawgroup_distribution_of_power has_law = law_type:law_chiefdom is_country_type = decentralized } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_elder_council }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_landed_voting
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_landed_voting } has_global_variable = lawgroup_distribution_of_power has_technology_researched = democracy not = { has_law = law_type:law_chiefdom } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_landed_voting }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_wealth_voting
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting } has_global_variable = lawgroup_distribution_of_power has_technology_researched = democracy not = { has_law = law_type:law_chiefdom } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_census_voting
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_census_voting } has_global_variable = lawgroup_distribution_of_power has_technology_researched = democracy not = { has_law = law_type:law_chiefdom } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_census_voting }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_universal_suffrage
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage has_law = law_type:law_chiefdom } has_global_variable = lawgroup_distribution_of_power has_technology_researched = egalitarianism } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_anarchy
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_anarchy } has_global_variable = lawgroup_distribution_of_power has_technology_researched = anarchism has_law = law_type:law_cooperative_ownership } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_anarchy }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_single_party_state
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_single_party_state } has_global_variable = lawgroup_distribution_of_power has_technology_researched = political_agitation } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_single_party_state }
	}
	option = {
		name = lawgroup_citizenship#公民权
		trigger = { daoyu_activate_law_trigger = yes }
		set_global_variable = lawgroup_citizenship
	}
	option = {
		name = law_ethnostate
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_ethnostate } has_global_variable = lawgroup_citizenship has_technology_researched = nationalism } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_ethnostate }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_national_supremacy
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_national_supremacy } has_global_variable = lawgroup_citizenship } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_national_supremacy }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_racial_segregation
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_racial_segregation } has_global_variable = lawgroup_citizenship } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_racial_segregation }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_cultural_exclusion
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_cultural_exclusion } or = { has_law = law_type:law_racial_segregation has_law = law_type:law_multicultural } has_global_variable = lawgroup_citizenship } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_cultural_exclusion }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_multicultural
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_multicultural } has_global_variable = lawgroup_citizenship has_technology_researched = egalitarianism has_law = law_type:law_slavery_banned } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_multicultural }
	}
	option = {
		name = lawgroup_church_and_state#教会与国家
		trigger = { daoyu_activate_law_trigger = yes }
		set_global_variable = lawgroup_church_and_state
	}
	option = {
		name = law_state_religion
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_state_religion } has_global_variable = lawgroup_church_and_state } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_state_religion }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_freedom_of_conscience
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_freedom_of_conscience has_law = law_type:law_total_separation } has_global_variable = lawgroup_church_and_state has_technology_researched = rationalism } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_freedom_of_conscience }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_total_separation
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_total_separation } has_global_variable = lawgroup_church_and_state has_technology_researched = empiricism not = { has_law = law_type:law_theocracy } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_total_separation }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_state_atheism
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_state_atheism } has_global_variable = lawgroup_church_and_state has_technology_researched = empiricism not = { has_law = law_type:law_theocracy } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_state_atheism }
	}
	option = {
		name = lawgroup_bureaucracy#官僚体制
		trigger = { daoyu_activate_law_trigger = yes }
		set_global_variable = lawgroup_bureaucracy
	}
	option = {
		name = law_hereditary_bureaucrats
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_hereditary_bureaucrats } has_global_variable = lawgroup_bureaucracy } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_hereditary_bureaucrats }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_appointed_bureaucrats
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_appointed_bureaucrats } has_global_variable = lawgroup_bureaucracy } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_appointed_bureaucrats }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_elected_bureaucrats
		trigger = {
			scope:daoyu_target_country = { 
				not = { has_law = law_type:law_elected_bureaucrats has_law = law_type:law_autocracy has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy has_law = law_type:law_elder_council }
				has_global_variable = lawgroup_bureaucracy
			}
		}
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_elected_bureaucrats }
	}
	option = {
		name = lawgroup_army_model#军队类型
		trigger = { daoyu_activate_law_trigger = yes }
		set_global_variable = lawgroup_army_model
	}
	option = {
		name = law_peasant_levies
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_peasant_levies } has_global_variable = lawgroup_army_model } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_peasant_levies }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_professional_army
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_professional_army } has_global_variable = lawgroup_army_model has_technology_researched = military_drill } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_professional_army }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_national_militia
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_national_militia } has_global_variable = lawgroup_army_model has_technology_researched = mandatory_service } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_national_militia }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_mass_conscription
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_mass_conscription } has_global_variable = lawgroup_army_model has_technology_researched = enlistment_offices } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_mass_conscription }
	}
	option = {
		name = lawgroup_internal_security#国内安全
		trigger = { daoyu_activate_law_trigger = yes }
		set_global_variable = lawgroup_internal_security
	}
	option = {
		name = law_no_home_affairs
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_no_home_affairs } has_global_variable = lawgroup_internal_security } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_no_home_affairs }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_national_guard
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_national_guard } has_global_variable = lawgroup_internal_security has_technology_researched = law_enforcement } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_national_guard }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_secret_police
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_secret_police } has_global_variable = lawgroup_internal_security has_technology_researched = central_archives } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_secret_police }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_guaranteed_liberties
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_guaranteed_liberties } or = { has_law = law_type:law_right_of_assembly has_law = law_type:law_protected_speech } has_global_variable = lawgroup_internal_security } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_guaranteed_liberties }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		if = { limit = { daoyu_activate_law_trigger = yes } remove_variable = d_law_tec_730 }
		else = { daoyu_activate_law_effect = yes }
	}
	after = {
		if = { limit = { has_variable = d_law_tec_730 } hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.730 popup = yes } } }
		else = { hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.720 popup = yes } } }
	}
}
#经济
d_law_tec.750 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = LAWS
	desc = ECONOMY
	flavor = daoyu_laws_desc
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_ruler_speaking_to_people.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/leader_speaking_to_a_group_of_people"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { set_variable = d_law_tec_750 }
	option = {
		name = lawgroup_economic_system#经济体制
		trigger = { daoyu_activate_law_trigger = yes }
		set_global_variable = lawgroup_economic_system
	}
	option = {
		name = law_traditionalism
		trigger = {
			scope:daoyu_target_country = { 
				not = { has_law = law_type:law_traditionalism has_law = law_type:law_per_capita_based_taxation has_law = law_type:law_proportional_taxation has_law = law_type:law_graduated_taxation }
				has_global_variable = lawgroup_economic_system
			}
		}
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_traditionalism }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_interventionism
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_interventionism has_law = law_type:law_serfdom } has_global_variable = lawgroup_economic_system has_technology_researched = manufacturies } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_interventionism }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_agrarianism
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_agrarianism } has_global_variable = lawgroup_economic_system has_technology_researched = romanticism } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_agrarianism }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_industry_banned
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_industry_banned } has_global_variable = lawgroup_economic_system has_technology_researched = romanticism } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_industry_banned }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_laissez_faire
		trigger = {
			scope:daoyu_target_country = { 
				not = { has_law = law_type:law_laissez_faire has_law = law_type:law_serfdom has_law = law_type:law_proportional_taxation has_law = law_type:law_isolationism }
				has_global_variable = lawgroup_economic_system has_technology_researched = international_trade
			}
		}
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_laissez_faire }
	}

d_law_tec.800 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_technology
	flavor = acquired_technology_notification_group
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_airship.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_industry.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
		if = {
			limit = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
			random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.800 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_target_country#重新选目标
		trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.800 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_modify_no_target_country
		trigger = { not = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.810 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_modify_target_country
		trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.820 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_modify_our_country
		random_country = { limit = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		add_modifier = { name = daoyu_target_country days = 1 }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.820 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.10 popup = yes } }
	}
}
#科技
d_law_tec.810 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_technology
	flavor = daoyu_technology_desc
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_airship.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_industry.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
		if = {
			limit = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
			random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.810 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NO_OBJECTIVE#你未选择目标
		trigger = { not = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { d_law_tec.810 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_target_country#重新选目标
		trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { d_law_tec.810 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_modify_target_country
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.820 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.800 popup = yes } }
	}
}

		default_option = yes
	}

		set_global_variable = dy_west_slavic
	}

		name = RESIGN
		default_option = yes
		set_global_variable = dculo_10
	}
	after = {
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = dculo_10 } remove_global_variable = dculo_10 trigger_event = { id = dculo.10 popup = yes } }
		else = { trigger_event = { id = dculo.60 popup = yes } }
	}

#文化
dculo.70 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_r_cu } desc = law_cultural_exclusion }#文化排斥
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_a_cu } desc = law_multicultural }#文化多元
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_c_cu } desc = russification_modifier }#民族同化
		}
	}
	flavor = daoyu_cheat
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_london_center.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/london_center"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = dculo_70
		daoyu_primary_culture_count_effect = yes
		random_country = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = {
			if = {
				limit = { or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_r_cu has_global_variable = daoyu_c_cu } }
				random_character = { limit = { has_trait = daoyu_tool_man } save_scope_as = daoyu_tool_man }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { name = north_german trigger = { daoyu_r_a_c_cu_trigger = { CULTURE = "north_german" } } daoyu_r_a_c_cu_effect = { CULTURE = "north_german" } }
	option = { name = south_german trigger = { daoyu_r_a_c_cu_trigger = { CULTURE = "south_german" } } daoyu_r_a_c_cu_effect = { CULTURE = "south_german" } }
	option = { name = ashkenazi trigger = { daoyu_r_a_c_cu_trigger = { CULTURE = "ashkenazi" } } daoyu_r_a_c_cu_effect = { CULTURE = "ashkenazi" } }
	option = { name = dutch trigger = { daoyu_r_a_c_cu_trigger = { CULTURE = "dutch" } } daoyu_r_a_c_cu_effect = { CULTURE = "dutch" } }
	option = { name = flemish trigger = { daoyu_r_a_c_cu_trigger = { CULTURE = "flemish" } } daoyu_r_a_c_cu_effect = { CULTURE = "flemish" } }
	option = { name = wallonian trigger = { daoyu_r_a_c_cu_trigger = { CULTURE = "wallonian" } } daoyu_r_a_c_cu_effect = { CULTURE = "wallonian" } }
	option = { name = boer trigger = { daoyu_r_a_c_cu_trigger = { CULTURE = "boer" } } daoyu_r_a_c_cu_effect = { CULTURE = "boer" } }
	option = { name = alemannic trigger = { daoyu_r_a_c_cu_trigger = { CULTURE = "alemannic" } } daoyu_r_a_c_cu_effect = { CULTURE = "alemannic" } }

namespace = dcc
#选定国家
dcc.10 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = ai_goal_form_country
	flavor = daoyu_create_country_flavor
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = FRONTEND_SWITCH_COUNTRY#切换国家
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } trigger_event = { id = dcc.11 popup = yes } }
			else = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.12 popup = yes } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_become_a_nonexistent_country#变身不存在的国家
		set_global_variable = daoyu_become_a_nonexistent_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.40 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_create_a_nonexistent_country_controlled_by_AI#创建由AI控制的不存在的国家
		trigger = { not = { any_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.19 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_create_a_nonexistent_country_controlled_by_AI#创建由AI控制的不存在的国家
		trigger = { any_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } }
		set_global_variable = dcc
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } set_variable = daoyu_potential_target set_variable = dcc_owned }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.20 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.10 popup = yes } }
	}
}
#创建由AI控制的不存在的国家

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.10 popup = yes } }
	}
}
#切换国家
dcc.11 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = FRONTEND_SWITCH_COUNTRY
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } desc = daoyu_root_get_name } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } desc = FRONTEND_SWITCH_COUNTRY } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } desc = daoyu_target_country_get_name } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } desc = RELOAD } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } desc = MULTIPLAYER_LOBBY_NOT_READY } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
	option = {
		name = NO_OBJECTIVE#你未选择目标
		trigger = { not = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.11 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_target_country#移除目标国家
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.11 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.11 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_variable = daoyu_remove_all_modifiers
			daoyu_modifier_remove_modifier_effect = yes
			every_scope_general = {
				remove_trait = pillager remove_trait = surveyor remove_trait = defense_in_depth_specialist remove_trait = resupply_commander remove_trait = forest_commander remove_trait = plains_commander
				remove_trait = mountain_commander remove_trait = expert_artillery_commander remove_trait = expert_offensive_planner remove_trait = expert_defensive_strategist set_variable = daoyu_betrayal_will_die
				remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier
				remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier
				remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier
				remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier
			}
			daoyu_state_modifier_remove_modifier_effect = yes
			scope:daoyu_target_country = { remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_cheat
		}
		play_as = scope:daoyu_target_country
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.10 popup = yes } }
	}
}

				and = { has_variable = daoyu_page_02 var:daoyu_unit_count_var > 37 }
				and = { has_variable = daoyu_page_03 var:daoyu_unit_count_var > 55 }
				and = { has_variable = daoyu_page_04 var:daoyu_unit_count_var > 73 }
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_page_01 } remove_variable = daoyu_page_01 set_variable = daoyu_page_02 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_page_02 } remove_variable = daoyu_page_02 set_variable = daoyu_page_03 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_page_03 } remove_variable = daoyu_page_03 set_variable = daoyu_page_04 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_page_04 } remove_variable = daoyu_page_04 set_variable = daoyu_page_05 }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		set_global_variable = daoyu_220
	}
	after = {
		daoyu_unit_count_clean_effect = yes
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_220 } remove_global_variable = daoyu_220 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.220 popup = yes } daoyu_page_clean_effect = yes }
		else_if = { limit = { daoyu_page_turning_trigger = yes } trigger_event = { id = daoyu_transfer_to_another_formation.1 popup = yes } }
		else = { daoyu_page_clean_effect = yes trigger_event = { id = daoyu_transfer_to_another_formation.2 popup = yes } }
	}
}
